To address this,", "        we introduce a spatial relaxation in the evaluation metrics.", "    ", "         - Test that the spatially relaxed FDP is below a specified FDR threshold (0.1).", "         - Test that the statistical power is above a specified threshold (0.8).", "        \"\"\"", "    ", "        n_samples = 400", "        shape = (20, 20)", "        n_features = shape[1] * shape[0]", "
